563→\n   564→func (p *MockProvider) Stop() error {\n   565→\t// We intentionally don't lock in this one because the whole point of this\n   566→\t// method is to be called concurrently with another operation that can\n   567→\t// be cancelled. {\n   579→\tdefer p.beginWrite()()\n   580→\n   581→\tp.ReadResourceCalled = true\n   582→\tp.ReadResourceRequest = r\n   583→\n   584→\tif !p.ConfigureProviderCalled {\n   585→\t\tresp.Diagnostics = p.ReadResourceFn(r)\n   591→\t}\n   592→\n   593→\tif p.ReadResourceResponse != nil {\n   594→\t\tresp = *p.ReadResourceResponse\n   595→\n   596→\t\t// Make sure the NewState conforms to the schema.\n   597→\t\t// This isn't always the case for the existing tests.\n   598→\t\tschema, ok := p.getProviderSchema().ResourceTypes[r.TypeName]\n   599→\t\tif !ok {\n   600→\t\t\tresp.Diagnostics = resp.Diagnostics.Append(fmt.Errorf(\"no schema found for %q\", r.TypeName))\n   601→\t\t\treturn resp\n   602→\t\t}\n   603→\n   604→\t\tnewState, err := schema.Body.CoerceValue(resp.NewState)\n   605→\t\tif err != nil {\n   606→\t\t\tresp.Diagnostics = resp.Diagnostics.Append(err)\n   607→\t\t}\n   608→\t\tresp.NewState = newState\n   609→\t\tif resp.Identity.IsNull() {\n   610→\t\t\tresp.Identity = r.CurrentIdentity\n   611→\t\t}\n   612→\n   613→\t\treturn resp\n   614→\t}\n   615→\n   616→\t// otherwise just return the same state we received without the write-only attributes\n   617→\t// since there are old tests without a schema we default to the prior state\n   618→\tif schema, ok := p.getProviderSchema().ResourceTypes[r.TypeName]; ok {\n   619→\n   620→\t\tnewVal, err := cty.Transform(r.PriorState, func(path cty.Path, v cty.Value) (cty.Value, error) {\n   621→\t\t\t// We're only concerned with known null values, which can be computed\n   622→\t\t\t// by the provider.\n   623→\t\t\tif !v.IsKnown() {\n   624→\t\t\t\treturn v, nil\n   625→\t\t\t}\n   626→\n   627→\t\t\tattrSchema := schema.Body.AttributeByPath(path)\n   628→\t\t\tif attrSchema == nil {\n   629→\t\t\t\t// this is an intermediate path which does not represent an attribute\n   630→\t\t\t\treturn v, nil\n   631→\t\t\t}\n   632→\n   633→\t\t\t// Write-only attributes always return null\n   634→\t\t\tif attrSchema.WriteOnly {\n   635→\t\t\t\treturn cty.NullVal(v.Type()), nil\n   636→\t\t\t}\n   637→\n   638→\t\t\treturn v, nil\n   639→\t\t})\n   640→\t\tif err != nil {\n   641→\t\t\tresp.Diagnostics = resp.Diagnostics.Append(err)\n   642→\t\t}\n   643→\t\tresp.NewState = newVal\n   644→\t} else {\n   645→\t\tresp.NewState = r.PriorState\n   646→\t}\n   647→\n   648→\tresp.Identity = r.CurrentIdentity\n   649→\tresp.Private = r.Private\n   650→\treturn resp\n   651→}\n   652→\n   653→func (p *MockProvider) PlanResourceChange(r providers.PlanResourceChangeRequest) (resp providers.PlanResourceChangeResponse) {\n   654→\tdefer p.beginWrite()()\n   655→\n   656→\tif !p.ConfigureProviderCalled {\n   657→\t\tresp.Diagnostics = resp.Diagnostics.Append(fmt.Errorf(\"Configure not called before PlanResourceChange %q\", r.TypeName))\n   658→\t\treturn resp\n   659→\t}\n   660→\n   661→\tp.PlanResourceChangeCalled = true\n   662→\tp.PlanResourceChangeRequest = r\n   663→\n   664→\tif p.PlanResourceChangeFn != nil {\n   665→\t\treturn p.PlanResourceChangeFn(r)\n   666→\t}\n   667→\n   668→\tif p.PlanResourceChangeResponse != nil {\n   669→\t\treturn *p.PlanResourceChangeResponse\n   670→\t}\n   671→\n   672→\t// this is a destroy plan,\n   673→\tif r.ProposedNewState.IsNull() {\n   674→\t\tresp.PlannedState = r.ProposedNewState\n   675→\t\tresp.PlannedPrivate = r.PriorPrivate\n   676→\t\treturn resp\n   677→\t}\n   678→\n   679→\tschema, ok := p.getProviderSchema().ResourceTypes[r.TypeName]\n   680→\tif !ok {\n   681→\t\tresp.Diagnostics = resp.Diagnostics.Append(fmt.Errorf(\"no schema found for %q\", r.TypeName))\n   682→\t\treturn resp\n   683→\t}\n   684→\n   685→\t// The default plan behavior is to accept the proposed value, and mark all\n   686→\t// nil computed attributes as unknown.\n   687→\tval, err := cty.Transform(r.ProposedNewState, func(path cty.Path, v cty.Value) (cty.Value, error) {\n   688→\t\t// We're only concerned with known null values, which can be computed\n   689→\t\t// by the provider.\n   690→\t\tif !v.IsKnown() {\n   691→\t\t\treturn v, nil\n   692→\t\t}\n   693→\n   694→\t\tattrSchema := schema.Body.AttributeByPath(path)\n   695→\t\tif attrSchema == nil {\n   696→\t\t\t// this is an intermediate path which does not represent an attribute\n   697→\t\t\treturn v, nil\n   698→\t\t}\n   699→\n   700→\t\t// Write-only attributes always return null\n   701→\t\tif attrSchema.WriteOnly {\n   702→\t\t\treturn cty.NullVal(v.Type()), nil\n   703→\t\t}\n   704→\n   705→\t\t// get the current configuration value, to detect when a\n   706→\t\t// computed+optional attributes has become unset\n   707→\t\tconfigVal, err := path.Apply(r.Config)\n   708→\t\tif err != nil {\n   709→\t\t\t// cty can't currently apply some paths, so don't try to guess\n   710→\t\t\t// what's needed here and return the proposed part of the value.\n   711→\t\t\t// This is only a helper to create a default plan value, any tests\n   712→\t\t\t// relying on specific plan behavior will create their own\n   713→\t\t\t// PlanResourceChange responses.\n   714→\t\t\treturn v, nil\n   715→\t\t}\n   716→\n   717→\t\tswitch {\n   718→\t\tcase attrSchema.Computed && !attrSchema.Optional && v.IsNull():\n   719→\t\t\t// this is the easy path, this value is not yet set, and _must_ be computed\n   720→\t\t\treturn cty.UnknownVal(v.Type()), nil\n   721→\n   722→\t\tcase attrSchema.Computed && attrSchema.Optional && !v.IsNull() && configVal.IsNull():\n   723→\t\t\t// If an optional+computed value has gone from set to unset, it\n   724→\t\t\t// becomes computed. (this was not possible to do with legacy\n   725→\t\t\t// providers)\n   726→\t\t\treturn cty.UnknownVal(v.Type()), nil\n   727→\t\t}\n   728→\n   729→\t\treturn v, nil\n   730→\t})\n   731→\tif err != nil {\n   732→\t\tresp.Diagnostics = resp.Diagnostics.Append(err)\n   733→\t\treturn resp\n   734→\t}\n   735→\n   736→\tresp.PlannedPrivate = r.PriorPrivate\n   737→\tresp.PlannedState = val\n   738→\n   739→\treturn resp\n   740→}\n   741→\n   742→func (p *MockProvider) ApplyResourceChange(r providers.ApplyResourceChangeRequest) (resp providers.ApplyResourceChangeResponse) {\n   743→\tdefer p.beginWrite()()\n   744→\n   745→\tp.ApplyResourceChangeCalled = true\n   746→\tp.ApplyResourceChangeRequest = r\n   747→\n   748→\tif !p.ConfigureProviderCalled {\n   749→\t\tresp.Diagnostics = resp.Diagnostics.Append(fmt.Errorf(\"Configure not called before ApplyResourceChange %q\", r.TypeName))\n   750→\t\treturn resp\n   751→\t}\n   752→\n   753→\tif p.ApplyResourceChangeFn != nil {\n   754→\t\treturn p.ApplyResourceChangeFn(r)\n   755→\t}\n   756→\n   757→\tif p.ApplyResourceChangeResponse != nil {\n   758→\t\treturn *p.ApplyResourceChangeResponse\n   759→\t}\n   760→\n   761→\t// if the value is nil, we return that directly to correspond to a delete\n   762→\tif r.PlannedState.IsNull() {\n   763→\t\tresp.NewState = r.PlannedState\n   764→\t\tresp.NewIdentity = r.PlannedIdentity\n   765→\t\treturn resp\n   766→\t}\n   767→\n   768→\t// the default behavior will be to create the minimal valid apply value by\n   769→\t// setting unknowns (which correspond to computed attributes) to a zero\n   770→\t// value.\n   771→\tval, _ := cty.Transform(r.PlannedState, func(path cty.Path, v cty.Value) (cty.Value, error) {\n   772→\t\tif !v.IsKnown() {\n   773→\t\t\tty := v.Type()\n   774→\t\t\tswitch {\n   775→\t\t\tcase ty == cty.String:\n   776→\t\t\t\treturn cty.StringVal(\"\"), nil\n   777→\t\t\tcase ty == cty.Number:\n   778→\t\t\t\treturn cty.NumberIntVal(0), nil\n   779→\t\t\tcase ty == cty.Bool:\n   780→\t\t\t\treturn cty.False, nil\n   781→\t\t\tcase ty.IsMapType():\n   782→\t\t\t\treturn cty.MapValEmpty(ty.ElementType()), nil\n   783→\t\t\tcase ty.IsListType():\n   784→\t\t\t\treturn cty.ListValEmpty(ty.ElementType()), nil\n   785→\t\t\tdefault:\n   786→\t\t\t\treturn cty.NullVal(ty), nil\n   787→\t\t\t}\n   788→\t\t}\n   789→\t\treturn v, nil\n   790→\t})\n   791→\n   792→\tresp.NewState = val\n   793→\tresp.Private = r.PlannedPrivate\n   794→\tresp.NewIdentity = r.PlannedIdentity\n   795→\n   796→\treturn resp\n   797→}\n   798→\n   799→func (p *MockProvider) ImportResourceState(r providers.ImportResourceStateRequest) (resp providers.ImportResourceStateResponse) {\n   800→\tdefer p.beginWrite()()\n   801→\n   987→func (p *MockProvider) ValidateStateStoreConfig(r providers.ValidateStateStoreConfigRequest) (resp providers.ValidateStateStoreConfigResponse) {\n   988→\tp.Lock()\n   989→\tdefer p.Unlock()\n   990→\n   991→\tp.ValidateStateStoreConfigCalled = true\n   992→\tp.ValidateStateStoreConfigRequest = r\n   993→\n   994→\tif !p.ConfigureProviderCalled {\n   995→\t\tresp.Diagnostics = p.ValidateStateStoreConfigResponse != nil {\n  1000→\t\treturn *p.ValidateStateStoreConfigResponse\n  1001→\t}\n  1002→\n  1003→\tif p.ValidateStateStoreConfigFn != nil {\n  1004→\t\treturn p.ValidateStateStoreConfigFn(r)\n  1005→\t}\n  1006→\n  1007→\t// In the absence of any custom logic, we do basic validation of the received config against the schema.\n  1008→\t//\n  1009→\t// This is a no-op if the given state object is\n    23→// already at the latest version.\n    24→//\n    25→// If any errors occur during upgrade, error diagnostics are returned. In that\n    26→// case it is not safe to proceed with using the original state object.\n    27→func upgradeResourceState(addr addrs.AbsResourceInstance, provider providers.Interface, src *states.ResourceInstanceObjectSrc, currentSchema providers.Schema) (*states.ResourceInstanceObjectSrc, tfdiags.Diagnostics) {\n    28→\tif addr.Resource.Resource.Mode != addrs.ManagedResourceMode {\n    29→\t\t// We only do state upgrading for managed resources.\n    30→\t\t// This was a part of the normal workflow in older versions and\n    31→\t\t// returned early, so we are only going to log the error for now.\n    32→\t\tlog.Printf(\"[ERROR] data resource %s should not require state upgrade\", addr)\n    33→\t\treturn src, nil\n    34→\t}\n    35→\n    36→\t// Remove any attributes from state that are not present in the schema.\n    37→\t// This was previously taken care of by the provider, but data sources do\n    38→\t// not go through the UpgradeResourceState process.\n    39→\t//\n    40→\t// Legacy flatmap state is already taken care of during conversion.\n    41→\t// If the schema version is be changed, then allow the provider to handle\n    42→\t// removed attributes.\n    43→\tif len(src.AttrsJSON) > 0 && src.SchemaVersion == uint64(currentSchema.Version) {\n    44→\t\tsrc.AttrsJSON = stripRemovedStateAttributes(src.AttrsJSON, currentSchema.Body.ImpliedType())\n    45→\t}\n    46→\n    47→\tstateIsFlatmap := len(src.AttrsJSON) == 0\n    48→\n    49→\t// TODO: This should eventually use a proper FQN.\n    50→\tproviderType := addr.Resource.Resource.ImpliedProvider()\n    51→\tif src.SchemaVersion > uint64(currentSchema.Version) {\n    52→\t\tlog.Printf(\"[TRACE] upgradeResourceState: can't downgrade state for %s from version %d to %d\", addr, src.SchemaVersion, currentSchema.Version)\n    53→\t\tvar diags tfdiags.Diagnostics\n    54→\t\tdiags = diags.Append(tfdiags.Sourceless(\n    55→\t\t\ttfdiags.Error,\n    56→\t\t\t\"Resource instance managed by newer provider version\",\n    57→\t\t\t// This is not a very good error message, but we don't retain enough\n    58→\t\t\t// information in state to give good
